\"$\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif v := os.Getenv(s); v != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\treturn v\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tlogger.Warn(\"Empty environment variable\", \"name\", s)\n\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t})\n\t\tif newV != v.Value {\n\t\t\tlogger.Debug(\"External label replaced\", \"label\", v.Name, \"input\", v.Value, \"output\", newV)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Note newV can be blank. https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/11024\n\t\tb.Add(v.Name, newV)\n\t})\n\tif !b.Labels().IsEmpty() {\n\t\tcfg.GlobalConfig.ExternalLabels = b.Labels()\n\t}\n\n\tswitch cfg.OTLPConfig.TranslationStrategy {\n\tcase otlptranslator.UnderscoreEscapingWithSuffixes, otlptranslator.UnderscoreEscapingWithoutSuffixes:\n\tcase \"\":\n\tcase otlptranslator.NoTranslation, otlptranslator.NoUTF8EscapingWithSuffixes:\n\t\tif cfg.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme == model.LegacyValidation {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"OTLP translation strategy %q is not allowed when UTF8 is disabled\", cfg.OTLPConfig.TranslationStrategy)\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported OTLP translation strategy %q\", cfg.OTLPConfig.TranslationStrategy)\n\t}\n\tcfg.loaded = true\n\treturn cfg, nil\n}\n\n// LoadFile parses and validates the given YAML file into a read-only Config.\n// Callers should never write to or shallow copy the returned Config.\nfunc LoadFile(filename string, agentMode bool, logger *slog.Logger) (*Config, error) {\n\tcontent, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tcfg, err := Load(string(content), logger)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"parsing YAML file %s: %w\", filename, err)\n\t}\n\n\tif agentMode {\n\t\tif len(cfg.AlertingConfig.AlertmanagerConfigs) > 0 || len(cfg.AlertingConfig.AlertRelabelConfigs) > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"field alerting is not allowed in agent mode\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(cfg.RuleFiles) > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"field rule_files is not allowed in agent mode\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(cfg.RemoteReadConfigs) > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"field remote_read is not allowed in agent mode\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tcfg.SetDirectory(filepath.Dir(filename))\n\treturn cfg, nil\n}\n\nfunc boolPtr(b bool) *bool {\n\treturn &b\n}\n\n// The defaults applied before parsing the respective config sections.\nvar (\n\t// DefaultConfig is the default top-level configuration.\n\tDefaultConfig = Config{\n\t\tGlobalConfig: DefaultGlobalConfig,\n\t\tRuntime:      DefaultRuntimeConfig,\n\t\tOTLPConfig:   DefaultOTLPConfig,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultGlobalConfig is the default global configuration.\n\tDefaultGlobalConfig = GlobalConfig{\n\t\tScrapeInterval:     model.Duration(1 * time.Minute),\n\t\tScrapeTimeout:      model.Duration(10 * time.Second),\n\t\tEvaluationInterval: model.Duration(1 * time.Minute),\n\t\tRuleQueryOffset:    model.Duration(0 * time.Minute),\n\t\t// This is nil to be able to distinguish between the case when\n\t\t// the normal default should be used and the case when a\n\t\t// new default is needed due to an enabled feature flag.\n\t\t// E.g. set to `DefaultProtoFirstScrapeProtocols` when\n\t\t// the feature flag `created-timestamp-zero-ingestion` is set.\n\t\tScrapeProtocols: nil,\n\t\t// When the native histogram feature flag is enabled,\n\t\t// ScrapeNativeHistograms default changes to true.\n\t\tScrapeNativeHistograms:         boolPtr(false),\n\t\tConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB: false,\n\t\tAlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms:  false,\n\t\tExtraScrapeMetrics:             boolPtr(false),\n\t\tMetricNameValidationScheme:     model.UTF8Validation,\n\t\tMetricNameEscapingScheme:       model.AllowUTF8,\n\t}\n\n\tDefaultRuntimeConfig = RuntimeConfig{\n\t\t// Go runtime tuning.\n\t\tGoGC: getGoGC(),\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultScrapeConfig is the default scrape configuration. Users of this\n\t// default MUST call Validate() on the config after creation, even if it's\n\t// used unaltered, to check for parameter correctness and fill out default\n\t// values that can't be set inline in this declaration.\n\tDefaultScrapeConfig = ScrapeConfig{\n\t\t// ScrapeTimeout, ScrapeInterval, ScrapeProtocols, AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms, and ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB default to the configured globals.\n\t\tMetricsPath:       \"/metrics\",\n\t\tScheme:            \"http\",\n\t\tHonorLabels:       false,\n\t\tHonorTimestamps:   true,\n\t\tHTTPClientConfig:  config.DefaultHTTPClientConfig,\n\t\tEnableCompression: true,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultAlertmanagerConfig is the default alertmanager configuration.\n\tDefaultAlertmanagerConfig = AlertmanagerConfig{\n\t\tScheme:           \"http\",\n\t\tTimeout:          model.Duration(10 * time.Second),\n\t\tAPIVersion:       AlertmanagerAPIVersionV2,\n\t\tHTTPClientConfig: config.DefaultHTTPClientConfig,\n\t}\n\n\tDefaultRemoteWriteHTTPClientConfig = config.HTTPClientConfig{\n\t\tFollowRedirects: true,\n\t\tEnableHTTP2:     false,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultRemoteWriteConfig is the default remote write configuration.\n\tDefaultRemoteWriteConfig = RemoteWriteConfig{\n\t\tRemoteTimeout:    model.Duration(30 * time.Second),\n\t\tProtobufMessage:  remoteapi.WriteV1MessageType,\n\t\tQueueConfig:      DefaultQueueConfig,\n\t\tMetadataConfig:   DefaultMetadataConfig,\n\t\tHTTPClientConfig: DefaultRemoteWriteHTTPClientConfig,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultQueueConfig is the default remote queue configuration.\n\tDefaultQueueConfig = QueueConfig{\n\t\t// With a maximum of 50 shards, assuming an average of 100ms remote write\n\t\t// time and 2000 samples per batch, we will be able to push 1M samples/s.\n\t\tMaxShards:         50,\n\t\tMinShards:         1,\n\t\tMaxSamplesPerSend: 2000,\n\n\t\t// Each shard will have a max of 10,000 samples pending in its channel, plus the pending\n\t\t// samples that have been enqueued. Theoretically we should only ever have about 12,000 samples\n\t\t// per shard pending. At 50 shards that's 600k.\n\t\tCapacity:          10000,\n\t\tBatchSendDeadline: model.Duration(5 * time.Second),\n\n\t\t// Backoff times for retrying a batch of samples on recoverable errors.\n\t\tMinBackoff: model.Duration(30 * time.Millisecond),\n\t\tMaxBackoff: model.Duration(5 * time.Second),\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultMetadataConfig is the default metadata configuration for a remote write endpoint.\n\tDefaultMetadataConfig = MetadataConfig{\n\t\tSend:              true,\n\t\tSendInterval:      model.Duration(1 * time.Minute),\n\t\tMaxSamplesPerSend: 2000,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultRemoteReadConfig is the default remote read configuration.\n\tDefaultRemoteReadConfig = RemoteReadConfig{\n\t\tRemoteTimeout:        model.Duration(1 * time.Minute),\n\t\tChunkedReadLimit:     DefaultChunkedReadLimit,\n\t\tHTTPClientConfig:     config.DefaultHTTPClientConfig,\n\t\tFilterExternalLabels: true,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultStorageConfig is the default TSDB/Exemplar storage configuration.\n\tDefaultStorageConfig = StorageConfig{\n\t\tExemplarsConfig: &DefaultExemplarsConfig,\n\t}\n\n\tDefaultExemplarsConfig = ExemplarsConfig{\n\t\tMaxExemplars: 100000,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultOTLPConfig is the default OTLP configuration.\n\tDefaultOTLPConfig = OTLPConfig{\n\t\tTranslationStrategy: otlptranslator.UnderscoreEscapingWithSuffixes,\n\t\t// For backwards compatibility.\n\t\tLabelNameUnderscoreSanitization: true,\n\t\t// For backwards compatibility.\n\t\tLabelNamePreserveMultipleUnderscores: true,\n\t}\n)\n\n// Config is the top-level configuration for Prometheus's config files.\ntype Config struct {\n\tGlobalConfig      GlobalConfig    `yaml:\"global\"`\n\tRuntime           RuntimeConfig   `yaml:\"runtime,omitempty\"`\n\tAlertingConfig    AlertingConfig  `yaml:\"alerting,omitempty\"`\n\tRuleFiles         []string        `yaml:\"rule_files,omitempty\"`\n\tScrapeConfigFiles []string        `yaml:\"scrape_config_files,omitempty\"`\n\tScrapeConfigs     []*ScrapeConfig `yaml:\"scrape_configs,omitempty\"`\n\tStorageConfig     StorageConfig   `yaml:\"storage,omitempty\"`\n\tTracingConfig     TracingConfig   `yaml:\"tracing,omitempty\"`\n\n\tRemoteWriteConfigs []*RemoteWriteConfig `yaml:\"remote_write,omitempty\"`\n\tRemoteReadConfigs  []*RemoteReadConfig  `yaml:\"remote_read,omitempty\"`\n\tOTLPConfig         OTLPConfig           `yaml:\"otlp,omitempty\"`\n\n\tloaded bool // Certain methods require configuration to use Load validation.\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\n// This method writes to config, and it's not concurrency safe.\nfunc (c *Config) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tc.GlobalConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.AlertingConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.TracingConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tfor i, file := range c.RuleFiles {\n\t\tc.RuleFiles[i] = config.JoinDir(dir, file)\n\t}\n\tfor i, file := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n\t\tc.ScrapeConfigFiles[i] = config.JoinDir(dir, file)\n\t}\n\tfor _, c := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\tc.SetDirectory(dir)\n\t}\n\tfor _, c := range c.RemoteWriteConfigs {\n\t\tc.SetDirectory(dir)\n\t}\n\tfor _, c := range c.RemoteReadConfigs {\n\t\tc.SetDirectory(dir)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (c Config) String() string {\n\tb, err := yaml.Marshal(c)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"<error creating config string: %s>\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn string(b)\n}\n\n// GetScrapeConfigs returns the read-only, validated scrape configurations including\n// the ones from the scrape_config_files.\n// This method does not write to config, and it's concurrency safe (the pointer receiver is for efficiency).\n// This method also assumes the Config was created by Load or LoadFile function, it returns error\n// if it was not. We can't re-validate or apply globals here due to races,\n// read more https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/15538.\nfunc (c *Config) GetScrapeConfigs() ([]*ScrapeConfig, error) {\n\tif !c.loaded {\n\t\t// Programmatic error, we warn before more confusing errors would happen due to lack of the globalization.\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"scrape config cannot be fetched, main config was not validated and loaded correctly; should not happen\")\n\t}\n\n\tscfgs := make([]*ScrapeConfig, len(c.ScrapeConfigs))\n\tjobNames := map[string]string{}\n\tfor i, scfg := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = \"main config file\"\n\t\tscfgs[i] = scfg\n\t}\n\n\t// Re-read and validate the dynamic scrape config rules.\n\tfor _, pat := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n\t\tfs, err := filepath.Glob(pat)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// The only error can be a bad pattern.\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error retrieving scrape config files for %q: %w\", pat, err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, filename := range fs {\n\t\t\tcfg := ScrapeConfigs{}\n\t\t\tcontent, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\terr = yaml.UnmarshalStrict(content, &cfg)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, scfg := range cfg.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\t\t\tif err := scfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif f, ok := jobNames[scfg.JobName]; ok {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple scrape configs with job name %q, first found in %s\", scfg.JobName, f))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = fmt.Sprintf(\"%q\", filePath(filename))\n\n\t\t\t\tscfg.SetDirectory(filepath.Dir(filename))\n\t\t\t\tscfgs = append(scfgs, scfg)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn scfgs, nil\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n// NOTE: This method should not be used outside of this package. Use Load or LoadFile instead.\nfunc (c *Config) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error {\n\t*c = DefaultConfig\n\t// We want to set c to the defaults and then overwrite it with the input.\n\t// To make unmarshal fill the plain data struct rather than calling UnmarshalYAML\n\t// again, we have to hide it using a type indirection.\n\ttype plain Config\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// If a global block was open but empty the default global config is overwritten.\n\t// We have to restore it here.\n\tif c.GlobalConfig.isZero() {\n\t\tc.GlobalConfig = DefaultGlobalConfig\n\t}\n\n\t// If a runtime block was open but empty the default runtime config is overwritten.\n\t// We have to restore it here.\n\tif c.Runtime.isZero() {\n\t\tc.Runtime = DefaultRuntimeConfig\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, rf := range c.RuleFiles {\n\t\tif !patRulePath.MatchString(rf) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid rule file path %q\", rf)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, sf := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n\t\tif !patRulePath.MatchString(sf) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid scrape config file path %q\", sf)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Do global overrides and validation.\n\tjobNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, scfg := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\tif err := scfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif _, ok := jobNames[scfg.JobName]; ok {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple scrape configs with job name %q\", scfg.JobName)\n\t\t}\n\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tif err := c.AlertingConfig.Validate(c.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\trwNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, rwcfg := range c.RemoteWriteConfigs {\n\t\tif rwcfg == nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null remote write config section\")\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip empty names, we fill their name with their config hash in remote write code.\n\t\tif _, ok := rwNames[rwcfg.Name]; ok && rwcfg.Name != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple remote write configs with job name %q\", rwcfg.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err := rwcfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\trwNames[rwcfg.Name] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\trrNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, rrcfg := range c.RemoteReadConfigs {\n\t\tif rrcfg == nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null remote read config section\")\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip empty names, we fill their name with their config hash in remote read code.\n\t\tif _, ok := rrNames[rrcfg.Name]; ok && rrcfg.Name != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple remote read configs with job name %q\", rrcfg.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t\trrNames[rrcfg.Name] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GlobalConfig configures values that are used across other configuration\n// objects.\ntype GlobalConfig struct {\n\t// How frequently to scrape targets by default.\n\tScrapeInterval model.Duration `yaml:\"scrape_interval,omitempty\"`\n\t// The default timeout when scraping targets.\n\tScrapeTimeout model.Duration `yaml:\"scrape_timeout,omitempty\"`\n\t// The protocols to negotiate during a scrape. It tells clients what\n\t// protocol are accepted by Prometheus and with what weight (most wanted is first).\n\t// Supported values (case sensitive): PrometheusProto, OpenMetricsText0.0.1,\n\t// OpenMetricsText1.0.0, PrometheusText1.0.0, PrometheusText0.0.4\n\tScrapeProtocols []ScrapeProtocol `yaml:\"scrape_protocols,omitempty\"`\n\t// How frequently to evaluate rules by default.\n\tEvaluationInterval model.Duration `yaml:\"evaluation_interval,omitempty\"`\n\t// Offset the rule evaluation timestamp of this particular group by the specified duration into the past to ensure the underlying metrics have been received.\n\tRuleQueryOffset model.Duration `yaml:\"rule_query_offset,omitempty\"`\n\t// File to which PromQL queries are logged.\n\tQueryLogFile string `yaml:\"query_log_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// File to which scrape failures are logged.\n\tScrapeFailureLogFile string `yaml:\"scrape_failure_log_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// The labels to add to any timeseries that this Prometheus instance scrapes.\n\tExternalLabels labels.Labels `yaml:\"external_labels,omitempty\"`\n\t// An uncompressed response body larger than this many bytes will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tBodySizeLimit units.Base2Bytes `yaml:\"body_size_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many samples post metric-relabeling will cause the scrape to\n\t// fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tSampleLimit uint `yaml:\"sample_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many targets after the target relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrapes to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tTargetLimit uint `yaml:\"target_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many labels post metric-relabeling will cause the scrape to\n\t// fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelLimit uint `yaml:\"label_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this label name length post metric-relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelNameLengthLimit uint `yaml:\"label_name_length_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this label value length post metric-relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelValueLengthLimit uint `yaml:\"label_value_length_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// Keep no more than this many dropped targets per job.\n\t// 0 means no limit.\n\tKeepDroppedTargets uint `yaml:\"keep_dropped_targets,omitempty\"`\n\t// Allow UTF8 Metric and Label Names. Can be blank in config files but must\n\t// have a value if a GlobalConfig is created programmatically.\n\tMetricNameValidationScheme model.ValidationScheme `yaml:\"metric_name_validation_scheme,omitempty\"`\n\t// Metric name escaping mode to request through content negotiation. Can be\n\t// blank in config files but must have a value if a ScrapeConfig is created\n\t// programmatically.\n\tMetricNameEscapingScheme string `yaml:\"metric_name_escaping_scheme,omitempty\"`\n\t// Whether to scrape native histograms.\n\tScrapeNativeHistograms *bool `yaml:\"scrape_native_histograms,omitempty\"`\n\t// Whether to convert all scraped classic histograms into native histograms with custom buckets.\n\tConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB bool `yaml:\"convert_classic_histograms_to_nhcb,omitempty\"`\n\t// Whether to scrape a classic histogram, even if it is also exposed as a native histogram.\n\tAlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms bool `yaml:\"always_scrape_classic_histograms,omitempty\"`\n\t// Whether to enable additional scrape metrics.\n\t// When enabled, Prometheus stores samples for scrape_timeout_seconds,\n\t// scrape_sample_limit, and scrape_body_size_bytes.\n\tExtraScrapeMetrics *bool `yaml:\"extra_scrape_metrics,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// ScrapeProtocol represents supported protocol for scraping metrics.\ntype ScrapeProtocol string\n\n// Validate returns error if given scrape protocol is not supported.\nfunc (s ScrapeProtocol) Validate() error {\n\tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape protocol %v, supported: %v\",\n\t\t\ts, func() (ret []string) {\n\t\t\t\tfor k := range ScrapeProtocolsHeaders {\n\t\t\t\t\tret = append(ret, string(k))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tsort.Strings(ret)\n\t\t\t\treturn ret\n\t\t\t}())\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// HeaderMediaType returns the MIME mediaType for a particular ScrapeProtocol.\nfunc (s ScrapeProtocol) HeaderMediaType() string {\n\tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\tmediaType, _, err := mime.ParseMediaType(ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\treturn mediaType\n}\n\nvar (\n\tPrometheusProto      ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusProto\"\n\tPrometheusText0_0_4  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText0.0.4\"\n\tPrometheusText1_0_0  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText1.0.0\"\n\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText0.0.1\"\n\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText1.0.0\"\n\tUTF8NamesHeader      string         = model.EscapingKey + \"=\" + model.AllowUTF8\n\n\tScrapeProtocolsHeaders = map[ScrapeProtocol]string{\n\t\tPrometheusProto:      \"application/vnd.google.protobuf;proto=io.prometheus.client.MetricFamily;encoding=delimited\",\n\t\tPrometheusText0_0_4:  \"text/plain;version=0.0.4\",\n\t\tPrometheusText1_0_0:  \"text/plain;version=1.0.0\",\n\t\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1: \"application/openmetrics-text;version=0.0.1\",\n\t\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0: \"application/openmetrics-text;version=1.0.0\",\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultScrapeProtocols is the set of scrape protocols that will be proposed\n\t// to scrape target, ordered by priority.\n\tDefaultScrapeProtocols = []ScrapeProtocol{\n\t\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0,\n\t\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1,\n\t\tPrometheusText1_0_0,\n\t\tPrometheusText0_0_4,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultProtoFirstScrapeProtocols is like DefaultScrapeProtocols, but it\n\t// favors protobuf Prometheus exposition format.\n\t// Used by default by the \"scrape_native_histograms\" option and for certain\n\t// feature-flags like \"created-timestamp-zero-ingestion\".\n\tDefaultProtoFirstScrapeProtocols = []ScrapeProtocol{\n\t\tPrometheusProto,\n\t\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0,\n\t\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1,\n\t\tPrometheusText1_0_0,\n\t\tPrometheusText0_0_4,\n\t}\n)\n\n// validateAcceptScrapeProtocols return errors if we see problems with accept scrape protocols option.\nfunc validateAcceptScrapeProtocols(sps []ScrapeProtocol) error {\n\tif len(sps) == 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"scrape_protocols cannot be empty\")\n\t}\n\tdups := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, sp := range sps {\n\t\tif _, ok := dups[strings.ToLower(string(sp))]; ok {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"duplicated protocol in scrape_protocols, got %v\", sps)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err := sp.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"scrape_protocols: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tdups[strings.ToLower(string(sp))] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\nfunc (c *GlobalConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tc.QueryLogFile = config.JoinDir(dir, c.QueryLogFile)\n\tc.ScrapeFailureLogFile = config.JoinDir(dir, c.ScrapeFailureLogFile)\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\nfunc (c *GlobalConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error {\n\t// Create a clean global config as the previous one was already populated\n\t// by the default due to the YAML parser behavior for empty blocks.\n\tgc := &GlobalConfig{}\n\ttype plain GlobalConfig\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(gc)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tswitch gc.MetricNameValidationScheme {\n\tcase model.UTF8Validation, model.LegacyValidation:\n\tdefault:\n\t\tgc.MetricNameValidationScheme = DefaultGlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme\n\t}\n\n\tif err := gc.ExternalLabels.Validate(func(l labels.Label) error {\n\t\tif !gc.MetricNameValidationScheme.IsValidLabelName(l.Name) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%q is not a valid label name\", l.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !model.LabelValue(l.Value).IsValid() {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%q is not a valid label value\", l.Value)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// First set the correct scrape interval, then check that the timeout\n\t// (inferred or explicit) is not greater than that.\n\tif gc.ScrapeInterval == 0 {\n\t\tgc.ScrapeInterval = DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeInterval\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeTimeout > gc.ScrapeInterval {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"global scrape timeout greater than scrape interval\")\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeTimeout == 0 {\n\t\tgc.ScrapeTimeout = min(DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeTimeout, gc.ScrapeInterval)\n\t}\n\tif gc.EvaluationInterval == 0 {\n\t\tgc.EvaluationInterval = DefaultGlobalConfig.EvaluationInterval\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeNativeHistograms == nil {\n\t\tgc.ScrapeNativeHistograms = DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeNativeHistograms\n\t}\n\tif gc.ExtraScrapeMetrics == nil {\n\t\tgc.ExtraScrapeMetrics = DefaultGlobalConfig.ExtraScrapeMetrics\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeProtocols == nil {\n\t\tif DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeProtocols != nil {\n\t\t\t// This is the case where the defaults are set due to a feature flag.\n\t\t\t// E.g. if the created-timestamp-zero-ingestion feature flag is\n\t\t\t// used.\n\t\t\tgc.ScrapeProtocols = DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeProtocols\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Otherwise, we leave ScrapeProtocols at nil for now. gc.ScrapeProtocols != nil {\n\t\t// Only validate if not-nil at this point.\n\t\tif err := validateAcceptScrapeProtocols(gc.ScrapeProtocols); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%w for global config\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t*c = *gc\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// isZero returns true iff the global config is the zero value.\nfunc (c *GlobalConfig) isZero() bool {\n\treturn c.ExternalLabels.IsEmpty() &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeInterval == 0 &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeTimeout == 0 &&\n\t\tc.EvaluationInterval == 0 &&\n\t\tc.RuleQueryOffset == 0 &&\n\t\tc.QueryLogFile == \"\" &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeFailureLogFile == \"\" &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeProtocols == nil &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeNativeHistograms == nil &&\n\t\t!c.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB &&\n\t\t!c.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms &&\n\t\tc.BodySizeLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.SampleLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.TargetLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.LabelLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.LabelNameLengthLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.LabelValueLengthLimit == 0 {\n\treturn c.GoGC == 0\n}\n\ntype ScrapeConfigs struct {\n\tScrapeConfigs []*ScrapeConfig `yaml:\"scrape_configs,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// ScrapeConfig configures a scraping unit for Prometheus.\ntype err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t//nolint:staticcheck\n\tif model.NameValidationScheme != model.UTF8Validation {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"model.NameValidationScheme must be set to UTF8\")\n\t}\n\n\tswitch globalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme {\n\tcase model.LegacyValidation, model.UTF8Validation:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"global name validation method must be set\")\n\t}\n\t// Scrapeconfig validation scheme matches global if left blank.\n\tlocalValidationUnset := false\n\tswitch c.MetricNameValidationScheme {\n\tcase model.UnsetValidation:\n\t\tlocalValidationUnset = validation method specified, must be either '', 'legacy' or 'utf8', got %s\", c.MetricNameValidationScheme)\n\t}\n\n\t// Escaping scheme is based on the validation scheme if left blank.\n\tswitch globalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme {\n\tcase \"\":\n\t\tif globalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme == model.LegacyValidation {\n\t\t\tglobalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.EscapeUnderscores\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tglobalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.AllowUTF8\n\t\t}\n\tcase model.AllowUTF8, model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown global name escaping method specified, must be one of '%s', '%s', '%s', or '%s', got %q\", model.AllowUTF8, model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues, globalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme)\n\t}\n\n\t// Similarly, if ScrapeConfig escaping scheme is blank, infer it from the\n\t// ScrapeConfig validation scheme if that was set, or the Global validation\n\t// scheme if the ScrapeConfig validation scheme was also not set. This ensures\n\t// that local ScrapeConfigs that only specify Legacy validation do not inherit\n\t// the global AllowUTF8 escaping setting, which is an error.\n\tif c.MetricNameEscapingScheme == \"\" {\n\t\t//nolint:gocritic\n\t\tif localValidationUnset {\n\t\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme = globalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme\n\t\t} else if c.MetricNameValidationScheme == model.LegacyValidation {\n\t\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.EscapeUnderscores\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.AllowUTF8\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tswitch c.MetricNameEscapingScheme {\n\tcase model.AllowUTF8:\n\t\tif c.MetricNameValidationScheme != model.UTF8Validation {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"utf8 metric names requested but validation scheme is not set to UTF8\")\n\t\t}\n\tcase model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape config name escaping method specified, must be one of '%s', '%s', '%s', or '%s', got %q\", model.AllowUTF8, model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues, c.MetricNameEscapingScheme)\n\t}\n\n\tif c.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB == nil {\n\t\tglobal := globalConfig.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB\n\t\tc.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB = &global\n\t}\n\n\tif c.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms == nil {\n\t\tglobal := globalConfig.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms\n\t\tc.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms = &global\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, rc := range c.RelabelConfigs {\n\t\tif err := rc.Validate(c.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, rc := range c.MetricRelabelConfigs {\n\t\tif err := rc.Validate(c.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// MarshalYAML implements the yaml.Marshaler interface.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) MarshalYAML() (any, error) {\n\treturn discovery.MarshalYAMLWithInlineConfigs(c)\n}\n\n// ToEscapingScheme wraps the equivalent common library function with the\n// desired default behavior based on the given validation scheme. This is a\n// workaround for third party exporters that don't set the escaping scheme.\nfunc ToEscapingScheme(s string, v model.ValidationScheme) (model.EscapingScheme, error) {\n\tif s == \"\" {\n\t\tswitch v {\n\t\tcase model.UTF8Validation:\n\t\t\treturn model.NoEscaping, nil\n\t\tcase model.LegacyValidation:\n\t\t\treturn model.UnderscoreEscaping, nil\n\t\tcase v))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn model.ToEscapingScheme(s)\n}\n\n// ScrapeNativeHistogramsEnabled returns whether to scrape native histograms.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) ScrapeNativeHistogramsEnabled() bool proto.Marshal(req)\n   384→\tif err != nil {\n   385→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to marshal read request: %w\", err)\n   386→\t}\n   387→\n   388→\tcompressed := snappy.Encode(nil, data)\n   389→\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(compressed))\n   390→\tif err != nil {\n   391→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to create request: %w\", err)\n   392→\t}\n   393→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n   394→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Accept-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n   395→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/x-protobuf\")\n   396→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n   397→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"X-Prometheus-Remote-Read-Version\", \"0.1.0\")\n   398→\n   399→\terrTimeout := fmt.Errorf(\"%w: request timed out after %s\", context.DeadlineExceeded, c.timeout)\n   400→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeoutCause(ctx, c.timeout, errTimeout)\n   401→\n   402→\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Read\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n   403→\tdefer span.End()\n   404→\n   405→\tstart := time.Now()\n  410→\t}\n   411→\n   412→\treturn httpResp, cancel, start, nil\n   413→}\n   414→\n   415→// handleReadResponse processes the HTTP response and returns a SeriesSet.\n   416→func (c *Client) handleReadResponse(httpResp *http.Response, req *prompb.ReadRequest, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool, start time.Time, cancel context.CancelFunc) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   417→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n   418→\t\t// Make an attempt at getting an error message.\n   419→\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   420→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   421→\n   422→\t\tcancel()\n   423→\t\terrStr := strings.Trim(string(body), \"\\n\")\n   424→\t\terr := errors.New(errStr)\n   425→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"remote server %s returned http status %s: %w\", c.urlString, httpResp.Status, err)\n   426→\t}\n   427→\n   428→\tcontentType := httpResp.Header.Get(\"Content-Type\")\n   429→\n   430→\tswitch {\n   431→\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-protobuf\"):\n   432→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   433→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\", strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)).Inc()\n   434→\t\tss, err := c.handleSampledResponse(req, httpResp, sortSeries)\n   435→\t\tcancel()\n   436→\t\treturn ss, err\n   437→\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-streamed-protobuf; proto=prometheus.ChunkedReadResponse\"):\n   438→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   439→\n   440→\t\ts := NewChunkedReader(httpResp.Body, c.chunkedReadLimit, nil)\n   441→\t\treturn c.handleChunkedResponseImpl(s, httpResp, queries, func(err error) {\n   442→\t\t\tcode := strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)\n   443→\t\t\tif !errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n   444→\t\t\t\tcode = \"aborted_stream\"\n   445→\t\t\t}\n   446→\t\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\", code).Inc()\n   447→\t\t\tcancel()\n   448→\t\t}), nil\n   449→\tdefault:\n   450→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   451→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\", strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)).Inc()\n   452→\t\tcancel()\n   453→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported content type: %s\", contentType)\n   454→\t}\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→func (*Client) handleSampledResponse(req *prompb.ReadRequest, httpResp *http.Response, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   458→\tcompressed, err := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   459→\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response. HTTP status code: %s: %w\", httpResp.Status, err)\n   461→\t}\n   462→\tdefer func() {\n   463→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   464→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   465→\t}()\n   466→\n   467→\tuncompressed, err := snappy.Decode(nil, compressed)\n   468→\tif err != nil {\n   469→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response: %w\", err)\n   470→\t}\n   471→\n   472→\tvar resp prompb.ReadResponse\n   473→\terr = proto.Unmarshal(uncompressed, &resp)\n   474→\tif err != nil {\n   475→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to unmarshal response body: %w\", err)\n   476→\t}\n   477→\n   478→\tif len(resp.Results) != len(req.Queries) {\n   479→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"responses: want %d, got %d\", len(req.Queries), len(resp.Results))\n   480→\t}\n   481→\n   482→\treturn combineQueryResults(resp.Results, sortSeries)\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→// combineQueryResults combines multiple query results into a single SeriesSet,\n   486→// handling both sorted and unsorted cases appropriately.\n   487→func combineQueryResults(results []*prompb.QueryResult, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   488→\tif len(results) == 0 {\n   489→\t\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: nil, cur: 0}, nil\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\tif len(results) == 1 {\n   493→\t\treturn FromQueryResult(sortSeries, results[0]), nil\n   494→\t}\n   495→\n   496→\t// Multiple queries case - combine all results\n   497→\tif sortSeries {\n   498→\t\t// When sorting is requested, use MergeSeriesSet which can efficiently merge sorted inputs\n   499→\t\tvar allSeriesSets []storage.SeriesSet\n   500→\t\tfor _, result := range results {\n   501→\t\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   502→\t\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   503→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   504→\t\t\t}\n   505→\t\t\tallSeriesSets = append(allSeriesSets, seriesSet)\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\t\treturn storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(allSeriesSets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge), nil\n   508→\t}\n   509→\n   510→\t// When sorting is not requested, just concatenate all series without using MergeSeriesSet\n   511→\t// since MergeSeriesSet requires sorted inputs\n   512→\tvar allSeries []storage.Series\n   513→\tfor _, result := range results {\n   514→\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   515→\t\tfor seriesSet.Next() {\n   516→\t\t\tallSeries = append(allSeries, seriesSet.At())\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   519→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\t}\n   522→\n   523→\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: allSeries, cur: 0}, nil\n   524→}\n   525→\n   526→// handleChunkedResponseImpl handles chunked responses for both single and multiple queries.\n   527→func (*Client) handleChunkedResponseImpl(s *ChunkedReader, httpResp *http.Response, queries []*prompb.Query, onClose func(error)) storage.SeriesSet {\n   528→\t// For multiple queries in chunked response, we'll still use the existing infrastructure\n   529→\t// but we need to provide the timestamp range that covers all queries\n   530→\tvar minStartTs, maxEndTs int64 = math.MaxInt64, math.MinInt64\n   531→\n   532→\tfor _, query := range queries {\n   533→\t\tminStartTs = min(minStartTs, query.StartTimestampMs)\n   534→\t\tmaxEndTs = max(maxEndTs, query.EndTimestampMs)\n   535→\t}\n   536→\n   537→\treturn NewChunkedSeriesSet(s, httpResp.Body, minStartTs, maxEndTs, onClose)\n   538→}\n   539→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. remoteapi.WriteMessageType\n\twriteCompression remoteapi.Compression\n}\n\n// ClientConfig configures a client.\ntype ClientConfig struct {\n\tURL                   *config_util.URL\n\tTimeout bool\n\tAcceptedResponseTypes []prompb.ReadRequest_ResponseType\n}\n\n// ReadClient will request the STREAMED_XOR_CHUNKS method of remote read but can\n// also fall back to the SAMPLES method if necessary.\ntype ReadClient interface {\n\tRead(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error)\n\tReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error)\n}\n\n// NewReadClient creates a new client for remote read.\nfunc NewReadClient(name string, conf *ClientConfig, optFuncs ...config_util.HTTPClientOption) (ReadClient, error) {\n\thttpClient, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(conf.HTTPClientConfig, \"remote_storage_read_client\", optFuncs...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tt := httpClient.Transport\n\tif len(conf.Headers) > 0 {\n\t\tt = newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(conf.Headers, t)\n\t}\n\thttpClient.Transport = otelhttp.NewTransport(t)\n\n\t// Set accepted response types, default to existing behavior if not specified.\n\tacceptedResponseTypes := conf.AcceptedResponseTypes\n\tif len(acceptedResponseTypes) == 0 {\n\t\tacceptedResponseTypes = AcceptedResponseTypes\n\t}\n\n\treturn &Client{\n\t\tremoteName:            name,\n\t\turlString:             conf.URL.String(),\n\t\tClient:                httpClient,\n\t\ttimeout:               time.Duration(conf.Timeout),\n\t\tchunkedReadLimit:      conf.ChunkedReadLimit,\n\t\tacceptedResponseTypes: acceptedResponseTypes,\n\t\treadQueries:           remoteReadQueries.WithLabelValues(name, conf.URL.String()),\n\t\treadQueriesTotal:      remoteReadQueriesTotal.MustCurryWith(prometheus.Labels{remoteName: name, endpoint: conf.URL.String()}),\n\t\treadQueriesDuration:   remoteReadQueryDuration.MustCurryWith(prometheus.Labels{remoteName: name, endpoint: conf.URL.String()}),\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// NewWriteClient creates a new client for remote write.\nfunc NewWriteClient(name string, conf *ClientConfig) (WriteClient, error) {\n\tvar httpOpts []config_util.HTTPClientOption\n\tif conf.RoundRobinDNS {\n\t\thttpOpts = []config_util.HTTPClientOption{config_util.WithDialContextFunc(newDialContextWithRoundRobinDNS().dialContextFn())}\n\t}\n\thttpClient, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(conf.HTTPClientConfig, \"remote_storage_write_client\", httpOpts...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tt := httpClient.Transport\n\n\tif len(conf.Headers) > 0 {\n\t\tt = newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(conf.Headers, t)\n\t}\n\n\tif conf.SigV4Config != nil {\n\t\tt, err = sigv4.NewSigV4RoundTripper(conf.SigV4Config, t)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(h map[string]string, underlyingRT http.RoundTripper) *injectHeadersRoundTripper {\n\treturn &injectHeadersRoundTripper{headers: h, RoundTripper: underlyingRT}\n}\n\ntype injectHeadersRoundTripper struct {\n\theaders map[string]string\n\thttp.RoundTripper\n}\n\nfunc (t *injectHeadersRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tfor key, value := range t.headers {\n\t\treq.Header.Set(key, value)\n\t}\n\treturn t.RoundTripper.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nconst defaultBackoff = 0\n\ntype RecoverableError struct {\n\terror\n\tretryAfter model.Duration\n}\n\n// Store sends a batch of samples to the HTTP endpoint, the request is the proto marshalled\n// and encoded bytes from codec.go.\nfunc (c *Client) Store(ctx context.Context, req []byte, attempt int) (WriteResponseStats, error) {\n\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(req))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// Errors from NewRequest are from unparsable URLs, so are not\n\t\t// recoverable.\n\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, err\n\t}\n\n\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", string(c.writeCompression))\n\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", remoteWriteContentTypeHeaders[c.writeProtoMsg])\n\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n\tif c.writeProtoMsg == remoteapi.WriteV1MessageType {\n\t\t// Compatibility mode for 1.0.\n\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion1HeaderValue)\n\t} else {\n\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion20HeaderValue)\n\t}\n\n\tif attempt > 0 {\n\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Retry-Attempt\", strconv.Itoa(attempt))\n\t}\n\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, c.timeout)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Store\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n\tdefer span.End()\n\n\thttpResp, err := c.Client.Do(httpReq.WithContext(ctx))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// Errors from Client.Do are from (for example) network errors, so are\n\t\t// recoverable.\n\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, RecoverableError{err, defaultBackoff}\n\t}\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n\t}()\n\n\t// NOTE(bwplotka): Only PRW2 spec defines response HTTP headers. However, spec does not block\n\t// PRW1 from sending them too for reliability. Support this case.\n\t//\n\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n\t// Parsing error means there were some response header values we can't parse,\n\t// we can continue handling.\n\trs, _ := ParseWriteResponseStats(httpResp)\n\n\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 2 {\n\t\treturn rs, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Handling errors e.g. read potential error in the body.\n\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(io.LimitReader(httpResp.Body, maxErrMsgLen))\n\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"server returned HTTP status %s: %s\", httpResp.Status, body)\n\n\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 5 ||\n\t\t(c.retryOnRateLimit && httpResp.StatusCode == http.StatusTooManyRequests) {\n\t\treturn rs, RecoverableError{err, retryAfterDuration(httpResp.Header.Get(\"Retry-After\"))}\n\t}\n\treturn rs, err\n}\n\n// retryAfterDuration returns the duration for the Retry-After header. In case of any errors, it\n// returns the defaultBackoff as if the header was never supplied.\nfunc retryAfterDuration(t string) model.Duration {\n\tparsedDuration, err := time.Parse(http.TimeFormat, t)\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\ts := time.Until(parsedDuration).Seconds()\n\t\treturn model.Duration(s) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n\t}\n\t// The duration can be in seconds.\n\td, err := strconv.Atoi(t)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn defaultBackoff\n\t}\n\treturn model.Duration(d) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n}\n\n// Name uniquely identifies the client.\nfunc (c *Client) Name() string {\n\treturn c.remoteName\n}\n\n// Endpoint is the remote read or write endpoint.\nfunc (c *Client) Endpoint() string {\n\treturn c.urlString\n}\n\n// Read reads from a remote endpoint. The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\nfunc (c *Client) Read(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n\treturn c.ReadMultiple(ctx, []*prompb.Query{query}, sortSeries)\n}\n\n// ReadMultiple reads from a remote endpoint using multiple queries in a single request.\n// The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n// Returns a single SeriesSet with interleaved series from all queries.\nfunc (c *Client) ReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n\tc.readQueries.Inc()\n\tdefer c.readQueries.Dec()\n\n\treq := &prompb.ReadRequest{\n\t\tQueries:               queries,\n\t\tAcceptedResponseTypes: c.acceptedResponseTypes,\n\t}\n\n\thttpResp, cancel, start, err := c.executeReadRequest(ctx, req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn c.handleReadResponse(httpResp, req, queries, sortSeries, start, cancel)\n}\n\n// executeReadRequest creates and executes an HTTP request for reading data.\nfunc (c *Client) executeReadRequest(ctx context.Context, req *prompb.ReadRequest) (*http.Response, context.CancelFunc, time.Time, error) {\n\tdata, err := proto.Marshal(req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to marshal read request: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tcompressed := snappy.Encode(nil, data)\n\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(compressed))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to create request: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Accept-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", *Client) handleReadResponse(httpResp *http.Response, req *prompb.ReadRequest, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool, start time.Time, cancel context.CancelFunc) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n\t\t// Make an attempt at getting an error message.\n\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n\n\t\tcancel()\n\t\terrStr := \"application/x-protobuf\"):\n\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\", strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)).Inc()\n\t\tss, err := c.handleSampledResponse(req, httpResp, sortSeries)\n\t\tcancel()\n\t\treturn ss, err\n\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-streamed-protobuf; proto=prometheus.ChunkedReadResponse\"):\n\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n\n\t\ts := This accessToken is attached to the Authorization header while making requests.\n   371→func newTokenProvider(cfg *AzureADConfig, cred azcore.TokenCredential) (*tokenProvider, error) {\n   372→\tvar scopes []string\n   373→\n   374→\t// Use custom scope if provided, otherwise fallback to cloud-specific audience\n   375→\tif cfg.Scope != \"\" {\n   376→\t\tscopes = []string{cfg.Scope}\n   377→\t} tokenProvider, nil\n   391→}\n   392→\n   393→// getAccessToken returns the current valid accessToken.\n   394→func (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) getAccessToken(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {\n   395→\ttokenProvider.mu.Lock()\n   396→\tdefer tokenProvider.mu.Unlock()\n   397→\tif tokenProvider.valid() {\n   398→\t\treturn tokenProvider.token, nil\n   399→\t}\n   400→\terr := tokenProvider.getToken(ctx)\n   401→\tif err != nil {\n   402→\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Failed to get access token: \" + err.Error())\n   403→\t}\n   404→\treturn tokenProvider.token, nil\n   405→}\n   406→\n   407→// valid checks if the token in the token provider is valid and not expired.\n   408→func (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) valid() bool {\n   409→\tif len(tokenProvider.token) == 0 {\n   410→\t\treturn false\n   411→\t}\n   412→\tif tokenProvider.refreshTime.After(time.Now().UTC()) {\n   413→\t\treturn true\n   414→\t}\n   415→\treturn false\n   416→}\n   417→\n   418→// getToken retrieves a new accessToken and stores the newly retrieved token in the tokenProvider.\n   419→func (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) getToken(ctx context.Context) error {\n   420→\taccessToken, err := tokenProvider.credentialClient.GetToken(ctx, *tokenProvider.options)\n   421→\tif err != nil {\n   422→\t\treturn err\n   423→\t}\n   424→\tif len(accessToken.Token) == 0 {\n   425→\t\treturn
